< text>
I've been visiting the midtown hair studio for the last 6 or 7 years, and keep coming back!

They almost always have walk in availability, and seem to schedule staff around peak hours so the wait isn't long. I can always expect to sit with a familiar hairdresser, which is great because they remember what I like. Whenever I walk in I'm greeted like an old friend. The entire staff, particularly the owner Zim, are always very friendly and charming, and never fail to make you feel welcome.

The haircuts are great, and the prices are reasonable. I always leave satisfied and will keep coming back. Great neighborhood hair cut!</text>

< text>
I went to the Planing Mill today for lunch.  I got there about 1:45pm.  I looked through the menu and wanted to stay but the only other patrons were at the bar.  I change my mind and got a slice togo.  I took it to my car with a soda.  The Pizza was completely dried out.  The crust was hard on the bottom and thick and chewy in the middle.  The tip of the slice was pointing up.  The cheese was hard and completely dried out.  I returned to the Pizzeria and waited at the counter.  The cashier came back from the bar in a few minutes and I told her the Pizza was dried and old.  She went directly to the phone and started dialing.  She never looked at it or acknowledged anything.  I gave her back the Pizza and she said she was contacting her manager.  I decided just to leave.  She knew the pizza was old and dried up when she sold it to me.  Seriously $9.00 ($7.50 plus tip) for a slice that Costco ($1.50) would have thrown out.  More importantly they knew they gave me awful pizza and never apologized.  Don't bother there are plenty of good Pizzerias around don't support rotten service, I'm not the only one who have seen this.< /text>

<review>Went here with a group of 10. The hostess was nice and friendly. We didn't have much if a wait but it was a Wednesday evening and there were graduation groups eating there at the time.
SERVICE: The service was pretty good. She took our drink orders right away and we got the drinks quickly. My complaint here is that the server didn't come back after we got our drinks to ask about refills on our beers or sodas.
FOOD: The food was great too. I made a custom pizza and about half of our table got personal pizzas while the rest got a salad or sandwich. No complaints from the others in my group about their food. <user_id>117637145840751721927<//user_id>< name>

< review>
I went this afternoon with some friends.  I have been to the Planing Mill before and have always had wonderful food, and no issues with service before today.  My friends and I each ordered personal pizzas and drinks.  I ordered the Muscles from Brussels, with no bacon.  I had been planning on ordering this pizza since we decided where we would be having lunch.  It sounded awesome, and I have heard that Mike's Hot Honey is amazing. Unfortunately, when my pizza arrived, I was told that they were out of the honey.  I was visibly disappointed and told our server that the only reason I ordered that pizza was because of the honey.  She was incredibly polite and apologized, and I appreciate that, but I wish that I had been told before hand that they were out of the honey.  I 100% would have ordered a different pizza.  That particular pizza has only 6 toppings and now I'm down 2.  The server offered to bring me a different sauce on the side, but I wasn't sure what to order.  She suggested the aioli that is typically paired with the appetizers.  I don't know that that was the right choice.  As I said, the server was very sweet, and very apologetic, my issue is that I felt like I was being offered a substutution for an ingredient, but there was no offer to "make it right" or make sure I was satisfied with what I got.  Other establishments would have offered a replacement, or perhaps a discount on my next visit, something....  But that was not the case.  Additionally, when we went to the bar, we were interested in trying the Mexican lager that was on the $2 Taco Tuesday special, but the bartender wasn't happy with the way it was pouring, so we were offered a different beer, at the same price.  The second beer wasn't as good, but for $2 it was a decent replacement.  This was the offer to make it right that I had hoped for with the pizza.  I will definitely be back, but I will be sure to ask if all the ingredients are available before I order my pizza.< /review>
